Recent Panic in the North

Bomb Explodes in a Prosperous and Bustling City

Decision Made to Intensify Martial Law Immediately

Secret Activities Discovered Near Tianjin

Tianjin Dispatch: The landmine discovered at the No. 25 overpass between Tianjin North Warehouse on the Beimi Road has been detailed in yesterday's dispatch. At around 10 PM that night, a thunderous sound was suddenly heard in the Southern City area, shaking the roofs and tiles. The citizens, already disturbed by rumors and in a state of panic, upon hearing the sudden loud noise, suspected a major event and scattered in all directions. Businesses closed their doors one after another. The military, police, and constabulary were all mobilized to guard the intersections and block traffic, conducting extensive searches. Upon investigation, it was found that the loud noise originated from a pile of dirty soil (i.e., what Shanghainese call a garbage can) in the No. 29 Hutong of Dongxingli. There were signs of the surrounding walls being damaged by a bomb blast (this hutong is full of brothels). However, no one was injured. As a result, three suspects were captured and are being secretly interrogated at the Public Security Bureau. Their names are not being released. It is only known that all three are staying at Room 42 of the Zhongdong Inn on Dongma Road. Emblems, letters of appointment, and secret telegrams were found in their room. There is no doubt that they are involved in political activities. According to the investigation by the Special Service Team, the landmine on the Beining Road that day and the bomb at night were all premeditated plans to create a terrifying atmosphere. On the afternoon of the 19th, the military, police, and constabulary authorities held a joint meeting and decided to intensify martial law immediately. The area north of the Hai River will be guarded by the 83rd Regiment of the 10th Army, and the area south of the river will be guarded by the 30th Regiment of the 4th Army. Other areas, such as the New Three-No-Zone, Xikai, Guangkai, and outside the railway, will be jointly guarded by the Public Security Bureau and the Gendarmerie Headquarters. After 12 o'clock every night, anyone with suspicious behavior will be inspected, and traffic will be cut off after 1 AM until 5 AM the next morning. However, there are no longer any army troops stationed in the city. The aforementioned 30th and 83rd regiments have just been transferred back from the Tianjin-Pukou front line for replenishment. Furthermore, Yuan Qingzeng, commander of the garrison, issued a proclamation in accordance with the provisions of martial law, stating that anyone who spreads rumors to confuse the public, gathers crowds to incite disturbances, robs people and property, or disrupts order will be dealt with by military law. Assemblies, organizations, purchase of firearms, private possession of weapons, and printing of reactionary publications are prohibited. He concluded by saying that anyone who dares to violate these orders will be severely punished and will not be shown any leniency. The commander's words will be followed by the law.

In addition, there is another matter that is also a potential threat to the North. Recently, young people have frequently come to Tianjin to engage in secret activities, buying off scholars, bandits, and Red Spear Society members to take the opportunity to cause disturbances. Recently, various proclamations have been discovered in Nangong, Jizhou, and other counties. A secret agent of the Pinghan Railway North Section Guard Headquarters recently captured Wang Degong, who claimed to be a division commander, in Cizhou. He is a well-known leader of the local Red Spear Society. He confessed that his army is under the control of a certain Zhang, with Wang as the general commander. Wang buys off scholars and bandits and Red Spear Society members in the Jizhou and Nangong areas. Deputy Commander Liu buys off former Zhili-Lu Army remnants and bandits in the Cangzhou, Yanshan, and Qingyun areas. Deputy Commander Jiang recruits bandits in the Chahar and Suiyuan areas. Their organization is divided into seven routes. Lu, the commander of the third route, and the first division are lurking in the Shunde, Nanhe, Neiqiu, and Lincheng areas along the Pinghan Railway. The second division is in the Jiulongguan and Malingguan areas. The third division is in the Cheng'an, Yongnian, Handan, and Cixian areas (Wang Degong is the division commander of the third division). However, the names of the personnel in charge of each route are mostly unknown, and their locations are also erratic, etc. Taiyuan has now telegraphed the Hebei Provincial Government to instruct the county magistrates and public security bureau chiefs of each county to instruct the village heads and deputies to strictly prevent and arrest them. A generous reward will be given upon successful capture, it is said. (August 20th)

Zhang Xueliang's Recent Situation in Beidaihe

Shenyang Dispatch: Northeast Cultural Society members Shen Nengyi and Zou Xigu reported to the press the day before yesterday that Japanese news agencies are spreading rumors that Commander-in-Chief Zhang was in danger in Beidaihe. Similar rumors were also circulating in Tianjin, Shanghai, and other places. The Japanese are fabricating news like this. We immediately lodged a protest with the Japanese side and demanded strict suppression of these rumors. We have received many telegrams from Commander-in-Chief Zhang in Beidaihe and various other sources. Commander-in-Chief Zhang is in very good spirits in Beidaihe. The American Ford aircraft that came to visit a few days ago was flown to Beidaihe by the pilot on the 18th to see Commander-in-Chief Zhang. He will bring photos of Commander-in-Chief Zhang back to Shenyang within the next few days, it is said. According to reports, the pilot of the American Ford aircraft is the American Bliss, accompanied by Xu Shiying, the deputy commander of the Northeast Aviation Force. They each flew a plane from Shenyang on the morning of the 18th and arrived in Beidaihe at around 10 AM. They went to visit Zhang Xueliang. Zhang had just finished bathing, and his bathrobe was not yet removed. After greeting them, Zhang immediately said, "Please see, do I look like I have encountered an accident? I am as healthy as ever. Where do these rumors come from?" He then laughed loudly. He then wrote a long letter in his own hand and entrusted Bliss to deliver it to Rong Zhen, the director of the Border Defense Military Department, and Zang Shiyi, the chairman of the provincial government. The gist of the letter was that he was in excellent spirits here, exercised every morning, and had gained 85 pounds compared to two months ago. As soon as the train is running, he will return to Shenyang. Please don't worry. Bliss returned to Shenyang on the morning of the 19th, while Xu Shiying remained in Beidaihe and has not yet returned. Furthermore, Hao Gengsheng, the director of physical education at Northeast University, returned to Shenyang from Beidaihe the day before yesterday. He said that on the 13th in Beidaihe, he played tennis with Zhang Xueliang at the Zhang family's mansion. Hao and his wife, Ms. Gao Zizi, formed one team, while Zhang teamed up with Ms. Liang Peiyao. The score that day was six to five, with Hao's team winning. On the 15th, the two sides continued to play, and the result was seven to five, still with Hao's team winning. Hao left Beidaihe at 8 AM on the morning of the 16th to go to Tianjin and then return to Shenyang. Zhang Xueliang's younger brother, Xueceng, even personally went to the station to see him off. Since Hao only left Beidaihe on the morning of the 16th, the Japanese claim that an accident occurred on the 15th is undoubtedly a rumor. Zhang is in very good health and high spirits. He gets up very early every day, reads official documents, and then plays ball and swims, which has greatly improved his health compared to when he was in Shenyang. (August 20th)

Investigation of Japanese Fishing Vessels Trespassing in Our Territorial Waters

The Ministry of Agriculture and Mining previously sent a dispatch to the seven coastal provinces of Liaoning, Hebei, Shandong, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Guangdong to investigate and report in detail on the facts of Japanese fishing boats trespassing and fishing within our country's territorial waters. Currently, all provinces except Guangdong, Fujian, and Zhejiang have provided detailed replies. Excerpts are as follows:

Liaoning: On June 13th, 13 Japanese steamships were fishing beyond the boundary in the waters near the Xinmin area. Wang Jing, the bureau chief of Jin County, led the Sui and Liao Flying Dragon gunboats to pursue and capture the Japanese fishing boat Datong Maru. On July 19th, Sato used a petroleum engine fishing boat to fish south of Yangjia Daquan in the waters of Zhuanghe. He was caught and ordered to sign a pledge never to trespass again before being released. Countless other secretly trespassing Japanese ships could not be confirmed.

Hebei: In June, a Japanese electric trawler was fishing across the border in Linyu, damaging more than ten baskets of fishing hooks belonging to fishermen such as Guan Yun, resulting in significant losses. In addition, Japanese fishing boats expelled from the northeastern sea often secretly went to the Hebei sea to trespass and fish. After the provincial authorities took measures to stop them, Japanese fishing boats no longer came. It has not been possible to investigate other counties along the coast of the province that are often trespassed by Japanese fishing boats.

Jiangsu: Every year in mid-April (approximately the beginning of the third lunar month), Japanese fishing vessels, often more than twenty, regularly catch rice fish northwest of the Haijiao of Shengshan Island. By mid-October last year, seventeen or eighteen Japanese trawlers, such as the 85 Hakata Maru, were crisscrossing the area northeast of Huanao Mountain, at a depth of 30 to 38 fathoms, causing a sharp decrease in the fish population. The various Shanghai boats were greatly affected and had to move to the southeast of Sheshan Mountain and the northwest of Bird Mountain to fish. The Japanese boats followed them without any scruples.

Shandong: Japanese fishing boats occupy two bases for fishing in the Bohai and Yellow Seas: A. Qingdao; B. Dalian. In Dalian, there are more than 600 fishing boats, with names such as Heishan Maru, Nishimura Maru, Hayashima Maru, Donten Maru, and Gendoku Maru. In Qingdao, there are more than 100 fishing boats, with names such as Myogen Maru, Asahi Maru, Qingdao Maru, and Nimyo Maru. Every spring, when the fishing season is at its peak, fishing boats from both places appear in the Bohai and Yellow Seas. In recent years, as anti-Japanese sentiment has increased in various parts of our country, they have built several 5,000-ton transport ships specifically to protect their fishermen and transport fresh fish. Their scheming can be imagined. There are two Grade A fishing grounds along the coast of Shandong. One near Longkou has two habitats: one extends from 37 degrees 30 minutes north latitude to 52 minutes north latitude, and 119 degrees 40 minutes east longitude to 120 degrees 30 minutes east longitude; the other extends from 38 degrees 3 minutes north latitude to 39 degrees north latitude, and 118 degrees 10 minutes east longitude to 121 degrees 50 minutes east longitude. The one near Rizhao has one habitat, extending from 36 degrees 45 minutes north latitude to 35 degrees 20 minutes north latitude, and 119 degrees 45 minutes east longitude to 120 degrees 10 minutes east longitude. Every year in April and May, Japanese fishing boats go to both places to fish. Our coastal fishermen are unable to purchase modern fishing boats and can only use old-fashioned sailing boats to fish. The competition for profits, gains, and losses is self-evident. Looking at the reports from the four provinces, the encroachment of Japanese people on our country's fishing industry is truly a great loss to the national economy.

No Result for Eastern Railway Telegraph Rights

Harbin Dispatch: The dispute over the Eastern Railway telegraph rights, which began in June and July, has still made no progress in the current meeting. The three telegraph issues that the expert committee could not resolve, such as the amount of sovereignty fees, the amount of international connection fees, and the inspection of outbound telegrams, were decided by the expert committee to be handed over to the Railway Bureau to be forwarded to the board of directors for resolution. In order to shorten the meeting period, the expert committee began to discuss telephone issues during the board of directors' deliberation of the three matters. However, the Russian side insisted that the telephone issues could only be discussed after the telegraph issues were resolved, and that the telephone system must also be restored to its original state before discussions could begin. This is especially different from the Russian side's initial statement that they would only discuss asset issues. Therefore, the telegraph issue has not been discussed for a month, and the telephone issue has also been shelved. The Transportation Committee recently telegraphed Li Deyan to negotiate with the Chinese director of the Eastern Railway as soon as possible to find a solution. Yesterday, Li Deyan met with Li Shaokang, who said that the board of directors is in contact with the matter, and it is still difficult to predict the outcome. It is faintly heard that the Russian deputy director, Yemushanov, told the Chinese director that it would not be difficult to move the inspection of telegrams to after the telegrams are sent. The amount of international connection fees and sovereignty fees can also be negotiated to find a compromise. If the Chinese side does not persist in its prejudices, the Russian side will still find it difficult to agree. Based on this, the future of the meeting may be deadlocked for a long time. (August 20th)

Quick Letter from Wuhu

The Anhui Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee issued an order the day before yesterday, ordering all municipal and county executive and supervisory committees to stop their activities and wait for others to be sent to take over. Xie Yongcun has been sent to take over the Wuhu County Party Department, and County Magistrate Sun Gongming has been sent to take over the Municipal Party Department. The Municipal Party Department received the order yesterday.

In order to prevent the activities of reactionary factions, the Central Propaganda Department has sent Huang Geng to Wuhu to establish the Wuhu Postal and Telegraph Inspection Office. The military and government officials in Wuhu are also forming a Postal and Telegraph Inspection Office, consisting of the 6th District Bandit Suppression Command, the Municipal Administration Preparatory Office, the Public Security Bureau, and the County Government, for the sake of local security. The work will begin immediately.

The Wuhu Municipal Administration Preparatory Office created the "Sail Transport Rapeseed Public Welfare Donation" last year, which was originally of a temporary nature. The Wuhu General Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly petitioned the provincial government to order its cancellation, but has not been approved. However, the various business guilds believe that since the Municipal Administration Office has already collected municipal administration donations and has funds, there is no need to collect rapeseed donations again. They are requesting the General Chamber of Commerce to telegraph the provincial government again today, ordering the Wuhu Municipal Administration Office to exempt rapeseed donations in accordance with the original plan.

The 6th District Bandit Suppression Command believes that wounded officers and soldiers have contributed to the party and the country, but local thugs often seduce and collude with them, causing incidents that are detrimental to local security. Today, a proclamation was issued stating that anyone found to be colluding with wounded soldiers to cause trouble will be severely punished according to military law. (August 24th)

Songjiang

Water Police to Launch a Large-Scale Bandit Suppression Campaign: In the kidnapping case of the 23rd in Fengjing Chaonitan, the bandits numbered over 100, some carrying machine guns and all wearing gray cloth short shirts and trousers, resembling a military uniform. According to villagers, this group is part of the Taibao A Shu's band. They set out from Liujia Weir and other places and looted all the way through Qianxu, Luxiang, and Langxia. Their goal is to obtain both money and weapons. They intend to descend heavily on Taihu Lake and harass the various towns and villages bordering Jiangsu and Zhejiang. They are also buying off local hooligans and gangsters, spreading rumors to confuse the public. Those with some wealth are planning to move away, as if a great disaster is imminent. However, it is the time when farmland is waiting to be harvested, and there are reports of unrest everywhere. Local people are very worried. It is now learned that Fan Zhicheng, the captain of the Songjiang Provincial Public Security First Water Team, plans to launch a large-scale bandit suppression campaign. He has ordered Gong Guozhen, the squad leader of the Tinglin division, to be responsible for guarding the eastern route. Liu Zhigao, the squad leader of the Zhangyan division, is responsible for guarding Zhujing and the western Taihu Lake area. The Agricultural Department Sends a Delegate to Investigate Agricultural Affairs: The Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining recently announced that the various forms for the agricultural survey in the 19th year have been prepared and approved by the provincial government meeting. Yesterday, an order from the provincial department was forwarded by the county government, instructing the district chiefs of each district to take good care of the surveyor upon his arrival.

Fengxian

Gold Case Fine Cleared and Dismissed: It has now been learned that Chuanchuan Pinzhu, the chief of the Public Security Seventh Branch, was accused by a certain Zhang of embezzling the fine in the Jin Yuting tobacco case during his tenure as chief of the Second Branch. The county commissioner Lu Mengchen and the bureau commissioner Peng Zhaoxin investigated and found the accusation unsubstantiated. It is claimed that the case occurred on June 16th and was reported for investigation by the Gaoqiao police station. After Jin learned of the case, he entrusted someone to voluntarily go to the hospital to quit smoking and donated 120 yuan to the police station for summer yellow uniforms and repairs to the Gaoqiao police station. When the money was delivered, it coincided with the change of chiefs between the two branches, so the former chief transferred it to the new chief and noted it in the handover book, which was presented to the authorities for approval. The procedures were complete, and there was no embezzlement or fraud.

Change of Education District: The educational districts in this county were originally divided into four based on the rivers in each township. However, this has caused obstacles with the autonomous regions, so the bureau plans to re-divide the districts starting this year, with Districts 1 and 5 as the first education district, Districts 2 and 3 as the second education district, Districts 4 and 6 as the third education district, and Districts 7 and 8 as the fourth education district.

Husband Catches Wife in Adultery, Father-in-Law Falsely Accuses Son-in-Law of Injury: Gu Yinhuo, a farmer from Zhengyi No. 14 in Zhuanghang, was adopted by Lu San of the same area as his son since childhood and renamed Lu Qiusheng. He was then married to Lu San's daughter, Bao Yun, whose promiscuity was well known. This time, Qiusheng happened to return from farming and passed by the home of his neighbor, Gu San, when he suddenly saw his wife having an affair. He was immediately enraged and summoned three relatives and friends to capture the adulterer. However, the adulterer's brother, Gu Guitang, gathered a crowd to intercept them on the way, so in the end, they only managed to seize his wife. They reported the matter to the chief of the Public Security Eighth Branch. Unexpectedly, Lu San did not take heed of the incident but instead blamed Qiusheng for interfering. He faked an injury and attempted to falsely accuse him. Fortunately, the county government investigated and found that the case involved adultery, so it ordered the adulterer Gu Asi to be arrested and dealt with. It is now learned that the Public Security Bureau arrested the adulterer yesterday and sent him to the county for investigation. The allegations by the gentry Ruan Lintang and others that the budget for the Nantang River project in Nanqiao exceeded the original estimate and that the project has no value, and that they are still collecting river taxes, have been submitted to the provincial government for investigation by Zhou Jiuxu, the director of the Construction Bureau. The original Nanqiao Nantang River project budget audit committee will be convened for a public audit.

Initiation of a Joint Defense Conference of Five Counties: County Magistrate Shen Qing recently reported that because bandits are rampant, he initiated joint defense with Nan Hui, Jinshan, Shanghai, and Songjiang. The organization will be expanded to include a joint defense conference of five counties within the month. It is said that Shen County Magistrate has been designated to draft the most important points, which include joint investigation, recruitment of joint teams, and sharing of expenses.

Jinshan

Water Police Encircle Notorious Bandit: Taibao A Shu, a notorious bandit, has gathered hundreds of people and has been wreaking havoc in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The army and police have repeatedly searched and suppressed him, but because the bandits are wandering aimlessly, it has been impossible to eradicate them. Recently, these bandits dared to lead a crowd to cause trouble in Guojiawei and other places in Jinshan County, and killed the chief of the Public Security Branch and the district chief. It has now been learned that after the water police division heard the news, it immediately reported to the Songjiang First Team Headquarters. The team reported the matter to the Minhang Shanghai Provincial Public Security Second District Headquarters by telephone. After hearing the news, District Chief Chen immediately summoned his troops and ordered the Jinghu warship to raise fire. District Chief Chen personally led his troops and the captain of the Jinghu warship, Jiang Xintian, to set out to Shenjing Chuanlai Temple the day before yesterday to carry out a severe suppression and dispatched warships to encircle them.

Suzhou

Judgment of Appeal of Robbery: Wu Dajinzi, a major bandit from Taihu Lake, robbed the Feihong Xiaolun, which was traveling between Suzhou and Chenmu, on April 20 of last year, and kidnapped two passengers surnamed Huang and Jin. He took them to Shanghai and hid them at No. 24 Ladu Road. Later, the detectives of the Public Security Third District, led by Xu Fengshan, led detectives to join forces with the French Concession police to break into the bandit den and arrest Wu Dajinzi, Shi Zixiang, Wang Si, and other 14 men and women. Liu Ziyun escaped and was later arrested by Xu and handed over to Gong Guoliang, the district chief, for questioning. The government presented it to the province to be shot on the spot. After Wu Dajinzi was shot, Liu Ziyun, who had escaped, was arrested by the Shanghai police and escorted back to Wu County. He was sentenced to imprisonment on June 16 of this year. Liu appealed to the High Court, and Lin Dawen, the presiding judge of the First Criminal Tribunal, revoked the original sentence on the day before yesterday, and Liu Ziyun was sentenced to twelve years in prison for helping the bandits.

Water Police Strictly Prevent Lake Bandits Activities: According to recent information obtained by the Suzhou Water Public Security Third District, Taihu bandits, Liu Xueshi, Xiong Yaonan, Zhang Si, Wang Xiaoren, Wang Heshang, Xu Xiaoyou, Li Chaochun, and Zheng Youen, originally planned to occupy Wujiang with 500 people and invade Suzhou, and to contact the Haidao bandits in Bei Da An Gang. At the same time, 200 bandits from Zhangzhu Mountain, Yixing, will occupy Dongshan as a base. At the same time, the troops will destroy the traffic on the Beijing-Shanghai Road from Yangcheng Lake. These people were appointed by Zhou Fengqi as Mao Zilong as the master, Wu Shaowu as the deputy master, and Zhong Zhaokui as the commander of the Taihu Independent Guerrilla Brigade. The bandits have now been defeated in advance by the water police and are no longer a threat. District Chief Gong is now strictly preventing the Taibao A Xu from harassing DianShan Lake from the Jinshan Pinghu area.

Wujiang

Two-Province Long-Distance Telephone Connection: The County Construction Bureau was recently instructed by the provincial government to connect the Zhenze telephone in the county to Nanxun in Zhejiang Province to facilitate news. After receiving the order, the bureau sent workers to erect telephone lines to connect with Nanxun, which has been completed and put into service. The telephone fee is set at one corner and five minutes each time from Zhen to Xun, with two-thirds of the fee going to Jiangsu and one-third to Zhejiang. From now on, the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang will become more convenient.

Provincial Public Security Team Enters the Lake to Suppress Bandits: According to reports from the Provincial Water Public Security Team stationed in the county, there are bandits gathering in Taihu Lake. Last night (the 23rd), Squadron Commander Huai Runqing personally led the entire team of patrol boats to enter Taihu Lake to destroy the bandits.

Wuxi

Sericulture Case Villagers Plead at Night: The Huinong Sericulture Manufacturing Plant outside the Guangfu Gate of Xiyi Huinong Bridge has not yet applied for registration with the Department of Agriculture and Mining, but it has manufactured a large number of autumn silkworms, counterfeiting the Tiger Brand trademark of Dayou Seed Farm in an attempt to sell them. At the same time, it submitted a request to the Department of Agriculture and Mining to fraudulently apply for registration. The Department of Agriculture and Mining approved an order for the Sericulture Suppression Office stationed in Xiyi to investigate and respond for verification. Afterwards, Dayou Seed Farm learned that Huinong Sericulture Manufacturing Plant was counterfeiting its trademark and sued the department, requesting a thorough investigation.

The Department of Agriculture and Mining immediately ordered the Sericulture Suppression Office to conduct a thorough investigation. The office sent personnel to confiscate a large number of privately manufactured autumn seeds (a total of 2,960 sheets worth more than 5,000 yuan) from the Huinong Sericulture Manufacturing Plant and sent them to the Xiyu cold storage in Guangqin District for temporary storage to prevent hatching. Afterwards, Chen Xiangchun, the manager of the Huinong Seed Plant, claimed that the silkworm seeds already had designated customers and that the time for raising silkworms was approaching, so he continued to fraudulently request the Department of Agriculture and Mining to approve the registration in order to openly sell the silkworm seeds. However, at about 1:00 a.m. yesterday, hundreds of villagers claiming to be buyers suddenly pleaded with the Suppression Office, demanding that the confiscated silkworm seeds be returned, but were unable to obtain a receipt. Duan Qishan, the director of the Sixth Division in charge of the area, immediately led police officers to suppress them and reported it to County Magistrate Pan and Public Security Bureau Director Xu. County Magistrate Pan and others immediately dispatched a company of police to suppress them and Director Xu of the Public Security Bureau also personally went to suppress them and persuaded the villagers to disperse and return home to await the official solution. It is reported that Deputy Director Yi Jianding of the Suppression Office has sent someone to the province to ask Director He for instructions on how to deal with the matter.

Provincial Committee Comes to Xiyi to Secretly Investigate the Sun Case: Zhang Tong, Yang Chongyuan, and others in Xiyi previously claimed that former County Magistrate Sun Zuji did not make public the county and municipal funds he handled, and that he released a large number of prisoners on bail upon his departure. They submitted a report to the Provincial Government Civil Affairs Department, requesting that a delegate be sent to Xiyi for a thorough investigation. After receiving the report, the Provincial Government deemed that the allegations should be thoroughly investigated and sent a certain gentleman to Xiyi for investigation the day before yesterday. After arriving in Xiyi, the gentleman contacted County Magistrate Pan and Public Security Bureau Director Xu and reviewed the judicial files. It is said that he has found clues and will return to the province to report after staying for one or two days.

Changzhou

Notorious Bandit Zou Pigen Captured: Liu Yuanshan, a soldier in the Second Detachment of the Police Team stationed in Xixia, Wuyi, learned that the notorious bandit Zou Pigen was hiding in Yangtan Village, a village near Laogu Bridge in the northern township. On the evening of the 23rd, he personally led his troops and three patrol officers from the Public Security Fourth Branch to the address and arrested the criminal Zou. During the preliminary trial, Zou confessed that he was 21 years old and had joined the bandits last year. He repeatedly committed robberies and had two pistols, but he was unable to go out and commit crimes due to illness. The pistols were taken away by the bandit leader. Captain Liu immediately sent him to the city team headquarters on the 24th. He will be sent to the court for investigation in the next few days.

Two Robbers Apprehended at East Gate: Zhang Boyuan's home near Banzhang in the Sixth District of Wuyi was previously robbed and injured. On the 24th, Zhang Boyuan came to the city by boat from the countryside. On the way, he suddenly saw a passenger at the Dongzhiqiao area who was the same robber who had robbed him. The person saw Zhang Boyuan looking at him and showed a terrified expression. When the boat arrived at Changbu, the robber borrowed a companion to have lunch at a small restaurant in the east of the city. Zhang Boyuan immediately called the police and arrested him. He was escorted to the police team headquarters and then to the county court for questioning. The robber confessed his name as Wang Fengsheng and his companion as Chang Huanlin.

Zhenjiang

Zhenjiang Merchants' Request: Jiangbei Bandits Impact Zhenjiang's Cloth, Silk, Piece Goods, Oil, Sesame, Sugar, Incense, and North-South Sundries Industries - The Four Trade Associations Jointly Telegraphed the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce Yesterday

The telegram stated that the associations and their members have repeatedly reported that bandits in the Jiangbei region are rampant, causing merchants and travelers to hesitate, and severely impacting the city's finances. Zhenjiang's commerce relies heavily on wholesale from Jiangbei. During the annual autumn harvest, it is customary to collect payments. However, now Jiangbei bandits are taking advantage of the military unrest to disrupt the rear areas. The situation in Xinghua and Jianhu is particularly dire and spreading rapidly. The provincial forces suppressing bandits and police are already stretched thin. Some unscrupulous officials are even covering up the situation, leaving the people under bandit control feeling utterly hopeless. Furthermore, the members' debt collectors face numerous obstacles, trapped in towns and facing life-threatening dangers while traveling by boat or cart. Those who haven't been sent out are dissuaded by the news. Consequently, the debts owed to the various industries in Jiangbei are significantly affected. A thorough solution is necessary for relief, as this concerns the livelihoods of merchants and residents and the city's finances. Given the above situation, we cannot remain silent. Therefore, we urgently request your association to telegraph the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Bandit Suppression Headquarters of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Office, urging them to quickly dispatch capable troops and shallow-water naval vessels to eliminate the banditry along the Jiangbei coast within the shortest possible time to provide relief. We are extremely anxious.

The Chamber of Commerce's Response Regarding Rice Prices: The Suzhou People's Livelihood Office (Su Min Ting) previously noted that rice prices had fallen in various regions, but Zhenjiang's prices remained high, suggesting possible manipulation by unscrupulous merchants. It requested the Chamber of Commerce to conduct a thorough investigation. It is now reported that the Chamber of Commerce responded to the People's Livelihood Office, stating that Zhenjiang has never been a rice-producing area and usually relies on rice shipments from neighboring provinces. Changsha and Wuhu are the hubs for rice production, and the new rice has already entered the market, explaining the declining prices. In Zhenjiang, the new grain has not yet appeared on the market. However, recently, the high-quality white rice (gao bai tang) has fallen to around fifteen yuan per dan (a unit of dry measure), and the lowest quality has fallen to around eleven yuan per dan. Only the foreign Xian rice supply remains limited, keeping the price above twenty yuan per dan. It is expected that by early to mid-next month, when the new rice is fully on the market, the supply will be abundant, and rice prices will definitely decrease and not increase.

Yangzhou

Bandits Demand Exorbitant Ransom: The kidnapping and assault case in Aozijie, in this city, resulted in the bandits sending letters yesterday (the 23rd), demanding a ransom of five thousand yuan for the kidnapped Chen girl and eight hundred yuan for the kidnapped Zhang boy. They also specified demands from over two hundred households and shops in the area, totaling thirty-two thousand seven hundred yuan, with a deadline of five days for negotiation at Beigushan in Jiangbei, or they would set fire to the area.

Crackdown on Gambling Temporarily Subsides: All the circumstances regarding the Fourth Branch Bureau of the Public Security Department at the Xiannv Temple in the county suppressing gambling and destroying the bureau due to a crowd gathering, and the resulting shopkeepers' strike due to arrests, have been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that the shops reopened today (the 23rd), and Chairman Guan of the Chamber of Commerce has come to the city to negotiate and mediate with the Public Security Bureau regarding the gambling offenders and those who caused the disturbances.

New Commissioner of Customs Appointed in Yang-You: The newly appointed Commissioner of Customs for Yang-You, Zhou Ziheng, arrived in Yangzhou on the evening of the 22nd and took office on the 23rd. It is rumored that there will be some internal staff changes.

Jingjiang

Captured Notorious Bandit Killed While Trying to Escape: Since the county party headquarters began registering surrendered bandits, dozens of bandit leaders, including Fan Linsheng and Ding Laosi from the northern townships, have successively surrendered, willing to capture the remaining bandits to atone for their past crimes. The county party headquarters did not hold them accountable for their past actions and allowed them to perform meritorious service while still under punishment. Fan Linsheng and others discovered that notorious bandits Fan Diyi and Zhu Deqing were hiding near the Shanghai-Nanjing Road, and reported this to the county. The county commissioned Qu Lixi and requested them to go and apprehend them. Qu then dispatched Long Hua, two patrol officers from the Public Security Bureau, to assist in the arrest. On the 16th, they first went to Changzhou and Suzhou to investigate, but found nothing. On the 21st, they arrived in Wuxi from Suzhou and encountered bandits Fan and Zhu loitering at the Wuxi Railway Station. They were immediately apprehended and escorted back to the county government that night. According to their confession, bandits Dai Rushan and Cui Jincheng were hiding in the countryside, plotting wrongdoing. Qu immediately ordered them to act as informants and arrest them. That night, the two criminals Dai Rushan and Cui Jincheng were captured at Daijiatai outside the north gate. While escorting them to the county for trial, Fan Diyi and Zhu Deqing attempted to escape at Houjialong. They were immediately killed.

Rugao

Xueyao Elementary School Burned Down: Yesterday, dozens of bandits suddenly arrived at Xuejia Yao in Zhentao and burned down the entire Complete Elementary School. They then went to the home of Xue Huanqing, a resident of the area, looted it completely, and shot and killed Xue's daughter-in-law and eldest grandson before scattering.

Police and Militia Capture a Large Number of Bandits: The county police stationed at Laohu Zhuang, based on a confidential report that bandits were gathering in the Zhangjia Zhuang area, immediately dispatched a team and captured Zhao Wenzai and eight others, who confessed to being bandits. They were all escorted to the brigade headquarters for interrogation. The Lang Zhuang militia of the First District, based on a confidential report that bandit leader Yang Xiaoshan and others were gathering at Shao Yixin's house, holding a meeting to discuss dividing land, arson, and murder, dispatched a team accompanied by informants and captured them. Bandit leader Feng Shaodang was killed on the spot, and fifteen others, including Wang Tieer, were captured alive. The militia headquarters received the news and immediately dispatched a team to escort them to the headquarters for interrogation.

Danyang

Kidnappers Escorted to Danyang for Trial: The case of the kidnapping of Zhang Hebao's son from Yangjia Zhuang in the western townships has been solved by the Zhenjiang County Government detectives at Taiping Mountain in Xinfeng. The victim has been rescued. The Zhenjiang County Government has dispatched police to escort the kidnappers, Sun Youcai and Zhu Guiyou, to Danyang for trial. The case was heard in court yesterday by Judge Guan and the suspects were shackled and imprisoned.

General Store Robbed in the Northern Townships: The general store opened by Zhang Laosi in Jiepai Village in the northern townships was suddenly invaded by six or seven bandits armed with guns on the morning of the day before yesterday. They twisted Laosi, extorted silver dollars, and then looted extensively before leaving with their loot.

Jiangyin

Report on the Situation of Opposing the Operation of Automobiles in Jingjiang: The Director of the Construction Bureau, Mao Feng, following instructions from the Construction Department to investigate and report on the situation of automobiles operating from the riverside to the city in Jingjiang, submitted a report to the Construction Department yesterday, outlining the following reasons: (1) The fourteen-mile road from Baweigang to Tianhou Palace in Jiangjing Road is still weak, and the section from Tianhou Temple to Jingjiang City cannot be used for automobiles. Approximately 600 people travel back and forth daily. There were originally over a hundred small carts. After the operation of rickshaws (man-powered carriages) this spring, the cart pullers converted to rickshaws. There are currently fifty rickshaws and fifty small carts. After the automobiles began operating in July, the rickshaw and small cart business declined sharply. This is the reason for the opposition to the automobile operation. (2) The automobile operation is run by various government officials, and ordinary people who wished to add their shares to the venture could not. This is the second reason for the opposition. (3) The operators of the automobiles do not comply with the existing regulations. This is the third reason for the opposition. (4) The first company, Jitung Automobiles, prepared two automobiles and began trial operation without receiving approval from the department. This pursuit of profits led to similar actions. Sheng Zichun's third and Sheng Xiru's fourth automobiles successively began operating. It is said that other entrepreneurs will continue to follow suit. On the one hand, opposition is rising, and on the other hand, disputes are occurring. (5) The Jingjiang Laborers' Corps mentioned by Sun Kuisian has not been filed with the department, and local areas are not very familiar with it. (6) Currently, the Public Security and Construction Bureaus have jointly issued a notice ordering all vehicles to cease operation without obtaining a license from the department. This is a legitimate way to eliminate opposition and resolve disputes. Furthermore, from Jingjiang City, eighteen li north to Guangling, eighteen li west to Shengcitang, twelve li east to Gushan, and six li west from Baweigang to Luweigang are all important transportation routes. Among them, the routes to Guangling Town and Luweigang have many pedestrians. The existing roads are relatively wide and can be easily repaired and used for rickshaws and carts. This development will not only make transportation more convenient, but also adjust the livelihood of laborers. Selection and Appointment of District Chiefs: After the district chiefs of each district in the county were ordered by the department to go to the province for training, the vacancies were filled by the county government convening a District Chief Committee in accordance with the District Chief Selection Regulations. After review, twelve qualified candidates, including Gu Tongkai, were presented to the department for selection. The service areas of Li Dichens, Gu Tongkai, Liu Xinhu, Miao Jieshou, Liu Zaigeng, and Huang Baoquan were determined by the county and reported to the People's Livelihood Department for approval.

Juntai Pawnshop Sends Personnel to Investigate and Inventory Qingyang Branch: The Juntai Pawnshop in Qingyang, established in the twelfth year of the Tongzhi reign of the Qing Dynasty, has been in operation for 57 years. Recently, it has incurred debts of over 70,000 yuan to three silver firms and three money exchanges in Wuxi, including Baokang, Run Yongji, Run Ruichang, Run Ruiyu, Fuchang, and Shengyong Sheng, resulting in losses. Furthermore, internal and external employees colluded in fraudulent activities, making it impossible to salvage the situation. The Shanghai Pawnshop Owners' Association (Dian Dong Yi Fan Tang) has dispatched Zhao Libin, an accountant from the Sanxin Yarn Factory, to Cheng (Jiangyin) to Qingyang to investigate and inventory.

News of County Magistrate Li's Resignation: County Magistrate Li Lengwei, finding his duties difficult to handle, has reportedly submitted his resignation to the provincial authorities. It is rumored that the province is currently looking for a replacement, and there is talk of appointing Hong, the current secretary of the Construction Department of Zhejiang, to the position.

Fishermen Rescue Two Soldiers: The fishermen from the Huangshangang fishing boat, while crabbing near Changshan Island in the Yangtze River the night before last, heard cries for help from the reeds. They rowed over and rescued two people who appeared to be soldiers. When asked, they spoke in Cantonese, which was incomprehensible. They could not write. After repeated questioning, it was said that they were from Shantou, Guangdong, named Chen Jingjia and Ma Qingan. They were on a black warship and had an argument with their companions over a rice bowl, and three of them fell into the Yangtze River. One had already drowned. Later, local people sent them to the Yidu Bureau to arrange for their return to their hometown. Nephew Beats His Paternal Uncle to Death: Shi Quanyuan, a farmer from Wangjiatai and Shijatai in the Second District, had an argument with his nephew, Shi Hanchen, from Tangjiatai, at Yu Wenrong's teahouse on the day before yesterday, over a cloth shirt. Shi Hanchen kicked Shi Quanyuan in the lower abdomen, causing serious injury and death. The next day, the murderer was captured. Shi Hanchen had previously committed a banditry case and was released after sentencing. Yesterday (the 24th), his wife, Huang, reported the case to the county. Judge Yang will go to the village this morning to conduct an autopsy.

Militia Captures Bandits: The Zhouzhuang militia searched Luxiaorifeng Village the night before last (the 23rd) and captured Zhang Maoyun, Zhang Xibao, Zhang Wubao, Zhang Fuyun, Bian Shunrong, Zhou Rubao, and Fang Baocheng, who had already been convicted of counter-revolutionary crimes. All seven were escorted to the militia and will be sent to the county for trial today.

Nantong

Six Counties Clear Bandits in Stages: After a defense and suppression meeting, Nantong, Rugao, Taixian, Haimen, Jingjiang, and Taixing in Jiangbei decided to completely eliminate all bandits within their respective territories. Since the police and militia forces of each county were insufficient, and the provincial security regiment was difficult to allocate, they divided the areas and proceeded in stages. On the 24th, the temporary bandit suppression commander, Li Changjiang, arrived in Nantong from Rugao, concentrated his troops, and joined the local police force to search and suppress the bandit areas.

County Government Sets Deadline for Each District to Procure Weapons for Self-Defense: The bandit atmosphere in each district of Nantong is unstable.

Previously, a county-wide defense conference decided that each district should procure 100 to 200 firearms within one month for effective self-defense. The deadline has now passed. The county government has set a deadline of three days for each district to submit the funds collected to the county in order to compile and present them to the province for the issuance of firearms to establish defense regiments.

Strictly Prohibit Thugs from Causing Disturbances: Recently, there have been frequent incidents of thugs robbing and injuring people inside and outside the city. Around 10 p.m. on the 23rd, more than a dozen thugs caused trouble at the residences of singing girls in the southeast camp. The county government's Public Security Bureau and Guard Office are strictly investigating and prohibiting such activities.

Hangzhou

Electrical Bureau Builds Provincial Electrical Grid: The Zhejiang Provincial Electrical Bureau considers the electrical industry to be a primary public utility that has a significant impact on people's lives and industrial production. Although there are hundreds of electrical operators in Zhejiang Province's counties, cities, and towns, most are small-scale organizations. Due to limitations in both capital and talent, the equipment is often poor, and electricity generation costs are too high, which means that electricity supply is not widespread. To support local private electrical industries and eliminate the above shortcomings, the Bureau plans to build a provincial electrical grid and purchase electricity from the grid. The Bureau will be responsible for all power generation and transmission projects in the province, while the sale of electricity will be contracted by electrical operators in various regions. The "Outline of the Zhejiang Provincial Electrical Bureau's Plan to Build an Electrical Grid" and "Measures for Zhejiang Provincial Electrical Operators to Purchase Electricity from the Electrical Grid" drafted by the Bureau have been submitted to the Zhejiang Provincial Government and forwarded to the Central Construction Committee for approval and implementation.

Hangchang Road Opens in Sections: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau is completing the construction of the Hangchang Highway in sections. The Huachong to Zaoxi section opened on September 1st. The Zaoxi to Qian section is scheduled to open on October 1st. The Yuqian to Changhua section is expected to open around November 15th. The opening ceremony will be held after the entire road is open.

County Bureau Chief Exam to be Held: The Zhejiang Provincial Government believes that according to the County Organization Law, bureau chiefs such as the Education Bureau Chief, Finance Bureau Chief, and Construction Bureau Chief must pass an examination before being hired. As the establishment of county organizations in Zhejiang Province is approaching, it is necessary to hold the examination for bureau chiefs in advance. Therefore, a modified plan has been drafted and submitted for approval.

Xiaoshan

召集成立水利委員會蕭山縣政府前奉建段廳訓令迅即組織水利委員會並發下縣政府水利委員會規程一份其第二條規定以下列人員爲委員組織之（一）縣長（二）縣政府建設局局長或建設科科長（三）縣政府建設委員會代表一人（四）縣政府聘請縣黨部代表一人（五）由縣政府分别聘任縣有水利專門學識人員及熟悉當地水利情形者共三人至五人云杜縣長已於二十一日上午在縣府開會成立并討論一切進行事宜及聘任各委員

萧山县政府前奉建段厅训令，迅即组织水利委员会，并发下县政府水利委员会规程一份。其第二条规定以下列人员为委员组织之: (一) 县长；(二) 县政府建设局局长或建设科科长；(三) 县政府建设委员会代表一人；(四) 县政府聘请县党部代表一人；(五) 由县政府分别聘任县有水利专门学识人员及熟悉当地水利情形者共三人至五人。杜县长已于二十一日上午在县府开会成立，并讨论一切进行事宜及聘任各委员。

Mietang Killed, Seriously Injured and Died: In Xiaoshan, downstairs Chen Place outside the East Gate, a Dongyang mietang (bamboo weaving craftsman), Yan Fuxing, was previously killed and injured in the throat due to a rape case. He reported it to the Public Security Bureau. Wang Jianming, a Western doctor, was called in to treat him, but unexpectedly, the trachea was cut. Repeated surgery was ineffective, and he died on the 22nd. The murderer, Zhu Ahuan, was arrested by the county police, but he denied everything. It is currently being investigated whether Zhu is the murderer and whether it was motivated by jealousy.

Shaoxing

Urge Payment of Construction Public Bonds: The Shaoxing County Government yesterday received a telegram from the province stating that the county has already received 300,000 yuan in bonds for construction public bonds. All bond payments must be collected quickly and remitted immediately, as there is an urgent need for funds. Do not delay any longer. County Magistrate Tang ordered the heads of the Public Security Bureau to quickly investigate and urge each designated household to make full payment of the bond amounts to the county so that they can be remitted.

Chinese Expedition

Football Team Battles Bachen to a Draw Again

Two to Two...Twelfth Battle Report

(August 10, Batavi (Jakarta) Communication) After the Chinese Expedition Football Team lost to the Surabaya Selection Team, many believed that their 2-6 defeat to the Batavi Selection Team in the previous match was not due to a lack of strength but to bad luck. Therefore, many people requested the authorities to ask the two teams to play again to satisfy the public's desire. Today's (August 10) rematch has been realized.

Initial Disadvantage Reduces Audience Turnout - Since the

Expedition Team suffered a heavy defeat of two to six last time, although their triumphant return from Surabaya to re-compete with the Bachen team, they still failed to restore the enthusiastic support of people from all walks of life. Therefore, the audience on this day was significantly less than the previous time. The stands were mostly empty, and the standing area was not as crowded as before. It is said that the income was less than 10,000.

Expedition Enters Field at 4:30 - At 4:30 p.m. on this day, the

Expedition Team, led by Li Qiuguai, entered the field in high spirits. Although many players were ill or injured, they did not show fatigue. After entering the field, they tried out their legs and feet slightly. Then the Bachen team entered the field and also tried out their legs and feet slightly. At 4:40 p.m., Hong Junyuan, representing the Xinbasaha Flower Factory, presented a wreath to the captain of the Expedition Team. The referee, Mr. Boluo Hua, then blew the whistle to gather the teams. One saw

Mayor Kicks Off, Two Sides Engage in Fierce Battle - After the two sides arranged their lineups, at 4:45 p.m., the order to attack was given.

First, the Mayor of Bachen, Mr. Merlos, performed the kickoff ceremony, and then the fierce battle began. The center forward of the Bachen team received the ball and immediately led the army to attack, but was repelled by the defense line of the Chinese Expedition Team. The Chinese team counterattacked, passing the ball left and right, with a fierce momentum as if they were about to defeat the enemy before breakfast. Just three minutes into the battle (4:48 p.m.), the center back of the Bachen team, seeing that the enemy's momentum was fierce and difficult to resist, used illegal means and was penalized by the referee with a free kick. Although the route was good, the front line's charge was slow and ineffective. Then the Chinese Expedition Team returned with a vengeance, advancing from both sides. The Flying General repeatedly broke into the enemy's formation, and the opponent's gate was in danger. Within these ten minutes, the Bachen team was surrounded, and the water could not flow out. If the left side was blocked, it would come from the right. At 4:52 p.m., Li Qiuguai and Dai Center Forward coordinated and then broke through the formation alone. The opponent's goalkeeper came out to meet them. The ball touched Li Qiuguai and bounced inward, shooting at a slightly oblique angle and entering the net. After the players passed the ball out, the front line tried to counterattack, but was blocked by Little Black Coal and passed the ball to the front to score a goal.

Gui Cheng and Yu Tian Play the First Merit - At 4:55

Li Qiuguai received a ball from Little Black Coal and saw that the Flying General was in the best position and quickly passed it to the right. After the Flying General received it, he broke into the formation and went straight to the goal area. He slowly passed it inward, and Chen Yutian chased up and shot straight at the goal. The ball went into the net. The audience cheered and threw their hats, and the sound was like crazy drunkards. Then, in another battle, the Bachen team tried hard to counterattack in order to retaliate, attacking from the left and right and advancing from the front and rear.

Zhou's Iron Gate Saves the Dangerous Ball with a Punch - At exactly 5 p.m., right

winger An Nangde received reinforcements from the rear and went straight up along the side. He crossed the ball at a suitable point. The four forwards chased it together, and the left forward jumped up and headed the ball. The Iron Gate lifted his fist to save the danger. At 5:04 p.m., the Bachen team launched another attack. The left forward of the Chinese Expedition Team kicked the ball out of bounds by mistake and was penalized with a corner kick. No damage was done. Zhou's Iron Gate passed the ball out, and the forwards launched a large-scale counterattack. Li Qiuguai approached the goal and shot the ball on top of the goal, missing a good opportunity. During these ten minutes, the battle was intense, and both sides attacked and defended fiercely, so that the ball had no fixed direction. As soon as this side broke the encirclement, the other side was attacked by the enemy.

Head and Feet Panic, Good Opportunity Missed - The battle reached 5:10

At 11:00, the Bachen team's rear defense kicked the ball out of bounds, and a corner kick was awarded. The Flying General was the main kicker, and the landing point was excellent. The Dragon Gate was in chaos, rushing from east to west, but the ball still hovered in front of the Dragon Gate. You could use your head and I could use my feet, but no one could get in. It was really a pity. At 5:19, the Bachen team counterattacked, and the Chinese Expedition Team's defense was empty. Center forward Ya Weilin was able to drive straight in and shoot at the goal, but the ball went over the goal, missing another good opportunity.

Gui Cheng Opens the Way, Lin Jing Receives the Success - At 5:20

At 5:00, after Zhou's Iron Gate sent the ball out, General Cao broke through the formation along the side and attacked fiercely. He walked as fast as he could. The Bachen defenders could not catch up and went deep into the heart. Seeing that Center Forward Dai was chasing to a good point, he passed to the center. Center Forward Dai received it and forced the Dragon Gate to shoot hard at the corner of the gate. Ya Beituli could not rescue in time and it went into the net again. Applause continued to erupt. After that, the battle lasted only a few minutes, and the referee blew the whistle to end the first half. The Chinese Expedition Team was able to take a 2-0 lead.

Seek Revenge, Bachen Team Attacks Fiercely - At 5:35

The battle continued at the minute. Although the Bachen team had lost two goals, their anger was not quenched. They tried hard to take revenge and launched a large-scale attack with a burst of energy. The Chinese Expedition Team's defenders were busy defending, and dangerous balls frequently appeared in the Dragon Gate. Within these five minutes, the Bachen team surrounded them and were penalized with four corner kicks, but fortunately they did not lose any. At 5:43, after the Chinese Expedition Team broke the encirclement, Little Black Coal dribbled the ball alone and

counterattacked, charging through the formation like there was no one around. It was a pity that he did not succeed and only won a corner kick. After that, the Chinese Expedition Team launched another attack. General Cao was transferred to the right forward and drove straight in alone. At 5:45, he rushed into the Dragon Gate boundary and shot hard at the goal, but the ball was seized by the goalkeeper and failed to succeed. In the blink of an eye, the Chinese Expedition Team's rear defense was in a hurry again. The Bachen team connected on the left and right and went straight to the Dragon Gate.

Iron Gate's Quick Hands Turn Danger into Safety - At 5:46

Zhou's Iron Gate's quick hands and sharp eyes saved the ball and turned danger into safety. The Chinese Expedition Team counterattacked, and the five forwards passed and connected with each other very well.

Insufficient Strength, Difficult to Achieve Miraculous Success - At 5:47

Chen Yutian and Center Forward Dai passed to each other and were able to drive straight in, but it was a pity that they did not have enough strength and were caught up by the enemy, and failed to succeed. The Bachen team's goalkeeper passed the ball to the front, and the front line received the ball and counterattacked. Dabogong was not strong enough after his illness and could not cope as he wished, resulting in frequent dangerous balls. At 5:48, they were penalized with another corner kick, but fortunately no damage was done.

Ball Monster Yutian Both Missed Good Opportunities - At 5:50

Li Qiuguai dribbled the ball and counterattacked, approaching the Dragon Gate and shooting out of bounds again. At 5:53, Chen Yutian had the opportunity to shoot, but he delayed and turned it into a cake. After that, the battle between the two sides became more intense, and the charge and trap were very impressive.

Corner Kicks Continue, Inevitably One Loss - At 6:01

The Chinese Expedition Team was penalized with another corner kick. The landing was very good, but Dabogong was too calm and was snatched by the enemy's left forward first. Zhou's Iron Gate stepped forward to rescue, but the left forward jumped up and headed the ball into the net, and the corner kick was retaliated with a rescue. Then, in another battle, the Bachen team launched another attack. The Chinese Expedition Team's rear defense was not strong enough and struggled to cope.

A Draw Was Finally Reached in Five Minutes - At 6:06

The Chinese Expedition Team was penalized with another corner kick. The landing point was even better, and the left forward Fan Linan was not supervised and was headed into the net again. Therefore, a draw was created. After this draw, in order to seek the final victory, both sides attacked and defended fiercely, but due to the time limit, they were unable to achieve their wishes. At 6:15, the referee blew the whistle to end the game, and the result was a 2-2 draw.

Rotary Cup Semi-Finals, Fourth Act

China Wins the Finals Berth

Qiu Feihai and Lin Baohua Defeat Portugal in Two Battles

Will Compete Against England on the 29th

The Rotary Cup semi-finals in Shanghai ended yesterday. In the Portuguese singles, China won both matches, winning the finals spot with a score of 4-1. The final will be held against the United Kingdom starting on the 29th of this month to win the championship. A brief record of yesterday's two battles is as follows:

Six丨Two

(1) Qiu Feihai Six丨Zero Kanavaro

Six丨Zero

The Qiu-Kan battle started a little earlier. Qiu did not slack off from beginning to end. Kanavaro was able to play cautiously in the first set. However, Qiu's left and right shots were easy and sharp, and the old man ultimately failed, winning only two games. Qiu won the first set six to two. From the second set, Kanavaro showed his old strength and went crazy, but most of the balls flew outside the court or were thrown into the net, with very few successes. Qiu won two consecutive sets with six to zero and ended the game.

Six丨Three

(2) Lin Baohua Six丨Three Ke Lasha

Six丨Two

The Lin-Ke battle was not very exciting because the situation was relaxed and it was difficult to generate interest. Lin previously claimed that he had to hit three six-to-three scores with Ke Lasha, so that Ke Lasha could lose with dignity. The first two sets were indeed six to three, but at the end of the third set, Lin's balls were not powerful, but Ke was not competitive and could not return the ball, so he lost a game and the score was six to two, and the game ended.

The semi-finals have ended. The United Kingdom eliminated the United States, and Portugal was defeated by China. The two countries, China and the United Kingdom, entered the finals week and will continue the finals for four days from the 29th of this month to resolve this year's championship.

Grass Tennis Tournament

Chinese and Western Tennis Circles Reconcile

After the Shanghai Chinese and Western tennis circles broke up and reconciled, the interest in tennis became more intense. The Shanghai Open Doubles Championship organized by the Shanghai Sports Promotion Association has ended. The Rotary Cup is in progress, and the various competitions of the Shanghai Grass Tennis Club will also be launched in due course, such as the Robert Cup International Doubles Tournament, the Open Singles, and the Open Doubles. The Robert Cup is scheduled for September 5th, the doubles are scheduled for September 1st, and the battles are scheduled for September 15th. China has already participated in the Robert Cup. Once the competition starts, the French Chamber of Commerce will be lively again for a while.

Basketball

Men's and Women's Games are Unreasonable

Men are Strong and Women are Weak, Which Does Not Conform to the Principle of Promoting Sports: The National Sports Association Issues a Notice Rejecting the Borrowing of the Court: The Chinese National Sports Association issued a notice on the 26th, saying:

"In light of the fact that the physical structure of men and women is vastly different in strength and weakness, there is no possibility of confronting each other in a basketball game that is highly competitive. It is not allowed in women's physiology and does not conform to the original intention of sports promotion. Therefore, we hereby announce that we will reject any request to borrow the Chinese Basketball Hall to hold men's and women's games. We hope everyone will understand."

Hong Kong Table Tennis Champion Wins

Defeated Shanghai Jiande Team Last Night

Last night at 8 o'clock, the Hong Kong champion, Zhonghua Zhiqiang Table Tennis Team, competed against the Shanghai Jiande Association Table Tennis Team at the Jiande Association gymnasium on Fusheng Road. The event began with an opening speech by the liaison director, Mr. Lu Zhongqiu, followed by a report by Mr. Yu Binqi, who briefly stated that although the Hong Kong team's visit to Shanghai had been discussed with the National Federation in writing, it had not received the Federation's approval. Therefore, there were no adequate preparations for external engagements, and all matters could be addressed to Mr. Lu. Finally, the notary, Wu Maoqing, announced the match records, with Wang Weixi recording the following results:

Hong Kong Jiande Performance Wins

Chen Yinting, Li Chuanshu 1 | 3 Jiande

Mo Qinghuan, Zhou Jianwen 1 | 3 Jiande

Zeng Yingfu, Lu Xiulu 0 | 3 Jiande

Deng Yaopeng, Zhu Wenlin 0 | 3 Jiande

Huang Wuping, Lu Zhongqiu 1 | 3 Jiande

Brief Review of Skills: Chen Yinting is skilled in both attack and defense, but unfortunately, he is too old. Veteran Li Chuanshu is good at responding, but lost to Li due to insufficient strength. Zhou Jianwen, although relatively new to the table tennis world, is diligent in practice and determined to succeed, becoming a player for the Zhonghua team with a leap. His fast shots are indeed difficult for domestic players to counter. Lu Xiulu is one of the Zhonghua players and happened to face Shang Fengling, the captain of the Hong Kong team and captain of the Jiande team, which attracted much attention. In the end, Lu's skills and powerful shots prevailed, and although Zeng actively resisted, he was defeated by Lu's endless changes. Zhu Wenlin is a rising star in the table tennis world, suitable for both offense and defense, and thus achieved victory. Although Huang Wuping's skills are good, he lost to Lu Zhongqiu in a 1-3 defeat.

All-Japan Swimming Championships, Day 3

Continues to Set New Records

Tokyo, 25th (Japanese United Press) The third day of the All-Japan Swimming Championships began at 7 PM, with the following results:

400 Meter Final

First place: Makino; Second place: Yokoyama. Both broke the 1928 Summer Olympics record set by Peck by 1.6 seconds, setting a new world record of 4 minutes and 56 seconds.

50 Meter Backstroke

First place: Suzuki, 33.4 seconds; Second place: Hitoe, 33.8 seconds. Both are new Japanese records.

Women's 200 Meter Backstroke

First place: Maeyama, 3 minutes 12.4 seconds. This is also a new Japanese record.

Not far from the world record of 3 minutes 11 seconds held by Ms. von Aehren of Germany. The event concluded at 9:15 PM.

Japanese Track and Field Athletes Lose to France

(Dentsu, Paris, 24th) In the Franco-Japanese track and field competition held in Paris, France scored 57 points, and Japan scored 47 points. Japan lost. Among the eleven events, the Japanese athletes who won were: Javelin: Kousaku Sumiyoshi, 61.1 meters; High Jump: Iwanaga, 1 meter 50; Long Jump: Mikio Oda, 7 meters; Pole Vault: Shuhei Nishida, 3.8 meters.

The Shanghai City Education Bureau issued an order to city schools stating: "The first semester of the 19th year of the Republic is already underway. The previously compiled budget for each school for the 19th year may not be entirely accurate and must be recompiled to ensure accuracy and factualness. It is necessary to separately issue a budget table and an investigation table, which are attached to this document. Principals of each school are instructed to fill out two copies according to the format and submit them to the bureau before August 31 for review and verification. Minutes of the Shanghai County Education Bureau Meeting

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 163rd bureau meeting yesterday after the memorial week. Attendees included Director Shi, Supervisor Zhu, Zheng Guo, Ji Sun Tingfang, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Yang Huiming, Yao Wuchen, Xi Simu, Yao Xingshu, Cai Sheng, Wu Renda, and Yan Zhongguang. (2) Regarding the re-election of members of the Economic Audit Committee in accordance with regulations, the following resolution was made: (A) Issue separate letters to various agencies and schools requesting them to nominate personnel to be reported to the bureau by September 7. (4) Omitted. (5) Regarding the procedures for the Tangwan Elementary School to pilot the central district system, it was decided to submit a special report to the provincial department and notify the distributed schools. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Full Restoration of Shipping on the Upper Yangtze

Chinese Steamships Also Begin Operations

Shipping on the upper Yangtze River, which had been disrupted by communist disturbances, has been fully restored as the communists in Gan and Xiang have recently been defeated. Commercial shipping has resumed. The latest news is as follows:

Changsha Urges Immediate Shipment of Goods: Changsha Merchants in Distress

When the communists entered Xiang, they ordered Shanghai to cease transporting goods. Recently, order has gradually been restored, and all goods are in short supply due to the commercial devastation. To meet the needs of supply, telegrams have been sent to Shanghai daily urging the shipment of general merchandise to Xiang in order to revitalize the market. Recently, textiles, cotton yarn, hardware, sundry goods, and white sugar have been continuously loaded and shipped. Foreign steamships such as Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nissin, and Jiujiang are competing to transport these goods to Xiang, which are then transferred to ships in Hankou.

China Merchants Bureau Assigns Scheduled Ships:

The China Merchants Bureau's upper Yangtze River ships have been suspended for a long time. Now that the "Kuaile" (Happy Profit) ship has been returned and repaired, the bureau has decided to take advantage of the congestion of goods going to Hunan and the lifting of the ban on Hunan rice to resume shipping on the upper Yangtze River. The "Kuaile" ship will be dispatched directly and will only stop at Hankou and Shashi along the way. This resumption of service is effective from today.

Foreign Marines Return to Shanghai:

During the emergency in Changsha, Britain dispatched a unit of marines to Hankou, and the Japanese Navy Ministry sent three more destroyers to the upper reaches. Now that the overall situation has stabilized, the British troops have been withdrawn to Shanghai first. The "Yanagi" and "Kashi" destroyers dispatched by Japan have also been ordered to return to Shanghai and are expected to arrive today.

Chinese and Foreign Companies Add New Ships:

The Sanbei Company is adding two new ships to the upper Yangtze line, named "Hongli" (Great Profit) and "Hongzhen" (Great Fortune), each with a net tonnage of 700 tons. In order to start service on the Xiangyi line as soon as possible, the factory has been ordered to expedite construction and complete it by October. Jardine Matheson's "Baohe" ship is also being rushed to install cabins and will be ready to sail next month. Taikoo's second new ship, "Wuxue", will also be able to come to Shanghai in mid-October.

Rice Industry Leader

Discusses the Grain Situation

Price Trends Expected to Decline

Special District Cheap Rice Distribution Center to Open Soon

As rice prices in the city continue to decline, a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, believing that the grain issue is of great importance to the livelihood of ordinary people, visited Mr. Lu Wenlong, a leader in the rice industry, to inquire about future trends in rice prices. Mr. Lu provided a detailed account of the situation and the upcoming opening of the Special District Cheap Rice Distribution Center. His remarks are recorded below:

Efforts to Suppress Rice Prices: A Month Ago, Rice Prices in This City Were Soaring

A Month Ago, Rice Prices in This City Were Soaring. Not only were ordinary citizens unable to afford to cook, but even ordinary shops and factories were affected. At that time, the city's Social Affairs Bureau and various organizations tried various methods, first with investigations and then with price limits, but the results were not very effective. Finally, a centralized distribution method was used, in which the rice arriving daily at the Nanshi and Zhabei docks, where rice ships docked, was compiled and distributed by the Rice Dealers Association to various rice shops to prevent rice merchants from raising prices and manipulating the market, so that rice prices would not continue to rise. At the same time, I (Mr. Lu referring to himself) conducted a detailed investigation with the rice dealers and assured the Social Affairs Bureau that there would be no food panic in Shanghai within a month, and I also tried to order foreign rice as relief. This is a general outline of the past efforts to suppress rice prices.

Good Harvests Everywhere This Year: The Import of Foreign Rice Is Not a Fundamental Solution.

Good Harvests Everywhere This Year: The Import of Foreign Rice Is Not a Fundamental Solution. Even in Shanghai, the cost of importing foreign rice is more than 10 million yuan. Wouldn't it be heartbreaking to give so much money to others? Therefore, the fundamental solution must be a good domestic harvest. This year's rice-producing provinces have had excellent harvests. It is estimated that Hunan and Jiangxi provinces have both had 120% harvests. The rice production in Pudong has increased by 40% compared to previous years. Therefore, the price of Pudong rice was 21 yuan when the new grain came on the market and has now fallen to 18 yuan. Also, the area bordering Anhui and Nanjing, which is a producing area of indica rice, has also had a good harvest, with the price of rice falling from 16 yuan to 14 yuan. In short, based on the current situation, if there are no major storms or prolonged rain disasters within a month, this year's harvest will not only be 120%, but will also have 140%. It is foreseeable that rice prices will decline.

Situation of Cheap Rice Distribution: The Efforts of the Authorities and Enthusiastic People in Society to Hold Cheap Rice Distribution.

Situation of Cheap Rice Distribution: The Fundamentally Fall Of Rice Prices: Primarily attributed to this year's good harvest. In addition, authorities and enthusiastic people in society are making every effort to carry out the distribution of cheap rice which is also an important factor. As of now, ten cheap rice distribution centers have already been established. Recently, Mr. Yu Qiaqing also plans to raise 500,000 yuan to distribute 100,000 dan of cheap rice, with a planned loss of 5 yuan per dan. The implementation plan involves an appropriation of 250,000 yuan from the Ministry of Finance, and 125,000 yuan each from the municipal government and the Public Works Department. Currently, 125,000 yuan from the Public Works Department and 50,000 yuan from the municipal government have been received, totaling 175,000 yuan. The first order of 1,500 tons of rice, or 15,000 dan, has arrived in Shanghai. 12,000 dan will be distributed to the existing cheap rice distribution centers, and the remaining 3,000 dan will be distributed in the leased territories and special districts. The planned location is within the Tianhou Temple, and the price will be set at 380 wen per sheng, totaling about 13 yuan per dan, which is about 2 yuan cheaper than the market price per dan. The method of the special district cheap rice distribution center will be slightly different from other cheap rice centers. Other centers only distribute 5 sheng per person, but the special district will increase it to 5 dou per person. The purpose is to help general small shops, small factories, and small-scale catering businesses. It is expected to be implemented this Thursday or Friday.

Jin Li Yuan Wharf

The Problem of Proceeding with Arbitration

Si Ming Bank Has Agreed to Guarantee Timely Rental Payment - Guo Wen She Reports: The lease negotiation case between the China Merchants Bureau Jin Li Yuan Wharf and the French Catholic Church of the Three Virtues has been changed from diplomatic means to legal proceedings and then to arbitration. The lawyer Gao Shuo from the China Merchants Bureau's arbitration office and Mr. Yamina, the arbitrator from the Three Virtues Church, have already made contact. It is reported that the China Merchants Bureau must find a bank to guarantee the timely payment of rent before the arbitrators from both sides can officially begin the arbitration proceedings. Yesterday, Shen Zhongyi, the accounting section chief of the China Merchants Bureau, went to the Shanghai Si Ming Bank and contacted Mr. Sun Hengfu. The bank has agreed to guarantee the timely rental payment by the China Merchants Bureau. It is reported that future arbitration matters will completely abandon legal proceedings and will still use diplomatic means to request mediation from the French Consul General if necessary.
