Business News

The Sino-Western Pharmacy announces that this summer's weather is hot and prolonged, not only in our country, but also in Europe and America, where the heat exceeds one hundred degrees. Moreover, Shanghai, with its large population crowded into small houses, is naturally more prone to epidemics than other ports. As a result, the number of epidemic prevention fluid sold by this pharmacy on the Fourth Avenue has been quite large recently. In terms of bottles, over 76 million bottles have been sold, an unprecedented achievement. This does not include wholesale to other ports and other summer medicines, they say.

The Yantai Changyu Company announces that the Golden Star Brandy and red and white wines produced by this company are brewed purely from self-grown grape juice, without any impurities. After analysis and testing by major doctors, it has been proven to be a tonic for replenishing blood. Since Mr. Zhang Junjian took over last year, he has diligently improved the wines, making the color and taste even more perfect. The company's general agency is located in Longxing Lane, Tianjin Road. A large quantity of wines has been shipped to Shanghai for sale. Those who wish to become distributors in this city or agents in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Jiangxi, Anhui, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, and other provinces are offered extremely favorable terms, they say.

The Qihua Company on Nanjing Road announces that since the price reduction on August 20th, the business has been very crowded because the prices of various goods have been greatly reduced. In addition to selling cheongsam dress fabrics for one yuan in the silk and cloth section, each department has a special discount section. For example, two-pound water bottles are sold for 85 cents each, new style cups and saucers are 95 cents for four sets, and all foreign men's and women's boots and shoes are discounted by 15%. Athletic shoes are discounted by 20%. This is truly a groundbreaking initiative, they say.

The Wing On Company announces that since the price reduction the day before yesterday, business in all departments has increased significantly. The sales of Conklin fountain pens in the stationery department have been particularly high. Male and female customers are seen constantly surrounding the counters to purchase them. Because Conklin fountain pens are specially discounted during this major sale, the original price of 14 yuan and 40 cents per pen is reduced to 9 yuan and 85 cents, with a limit of 500 pens. Engraving is free. There are also loose-leaf lecture binders for 50 cents each, Chinese letter paper for 1 yuan and 10 books, newly packaged letter paper for 1 yuan and 7 books, American pencil sharpeners for 2 yuan and 30 cents each, top-quality ink colors for 60 cents each, this brand of crepe paper for 10 cents per bolt, German pencils for 30 cents per dozen, and two dozen packs of stationery and envelopes for 40 cents per box. Conklin pen prices range from 5 yuan and 95 cents to 8 yuan, 1 jiao, and 9 fen, with dozens of varieties, they say.

The Xinyuanxing Advertising Department announces that the "Double Knife" brand disinfectant, a domestic product, is well-known for its low price and high quality, and is sought after far and wide. Recently, the disinfectant was tested by the Industrial Products Testing Institute of the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau. The results showed that the disinfectant, diluted 60 times with water, can kill typhoid bacteria in two and a half minutes. Diluted 110 times with water, it can kill typhoid bacteria in fifteen minutes. Although the effectiveness of this disinfectant is generally known by users, this test proves that public confidence will be further strengthened, they say.

During each sale period, customers, recognizing that such opportunities are rare, create a very lively scene. This year, the variety of products is greater than last year. The liveliness of the sale period is expected to be even greater than last year, they say.

The name "Max Kay" is a combination of the words "Mask" and "Key," so these two objects are used as the trademark, which is very novel. Currently, tea, pastries, and candies are sold first. Social News

Chicago Almost Becomes an International City

Poles Alone Account for 400,000, Chinese Over 2,300

Chicago News: The recent statistics of the foreign population in Chicago have been completed. The Poles are the most numerous, increasing from 137,611 in 1920 to 400,000. The Germans are second, increasing from 112,283 in 1920 to 350,000. The Black population increased from 109,458 to over 200,000. Other increases include the Irish, from 56,786 to 175,000; the Swedes, from 58,563 to 175,000; the Italians, from 59,215 to 150,000; the Czechs, from 50,392 to 150,000; the Greeks, from 11,546 to 60,000; and the Danes, from 11,268 to 30,000. There are also 300 Japanese and 2,356 Chinese.

Japanese Promote the Use of Domestic Products

If the People Use Domestic Products as Much as Possible, 600 Million Yuan Can Be Saved Annually

Pay Attention to Quality and Price When Promoting Domestic Products

—A Good Example for Our People—

A translation from a Japanese magazine by the World News Agency states that the Japanese economy has fallen into a deep slump due to the postwar economic crisis and the Great Kanto Earthquake. The government is painstakingly seeking ways to break the current situation and believes that the only way is to promote domestic production to consolidate the foundation of the national economy and improve the balance of international payments. Therefore, there is a movement to use domestic products. The government has conducted extensive investigations on this matter. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry has compiled a book called "Survey of Domestic Products," which records the actual situation of domestic industries. On the one hand, it investigates the types of consumer goods, compares the types of domestically produced goods and imported goods item by item, and divides them into several categories, namely (1) those that must rely on foreign countries, (2) those that cannot be produced domestically, (3) those that have domestic products but are too expensive, (4) those that have domestic products but are of poor quality and not suitable for use, and (5) those with other special circumstances. Experts conduct detailed reviews and comparisons of each category of goods, and the results are surprising to the experts, as many imported goods can be replaced by Japanese domestic products.

The following table lists seven categories of imported goods that can be replaced by Japanese goods, and the total value (in Japanese yen) of imports to Japan in the most recent three years:

1929

47,009,315 119,693,523 144,294,890 136,068,123 41,023,457 10,583,205 102,364,375 601,306,888 2,136,240,015 27%

1928

70,551,035 131,910,332 135,955,198 138,087,303 40,375,775 8,771,589 127,840,774 650,314,995 2,196,314,727 30%

1927

84,688,800 122,985,543 107,220,332 129,557,153 46,267,926 7,770,943 118,209,939 616,700,636 2,179,153,858

28%

Metal Products

Chemical Products

Beverages and Food

Total

Total Imports

Ratio of Total of 7 Items to Total Value

From the above table, it can be seen that if the people purchase domestic products as much as possible, at least 600 million yen a year can be saved out of the total import value of 2.1 billion or 2.2 billion yen, and this amount of 600 million yen a year can enrich the country. The importance of the meaning of the people using domestic products can be seen. The above seven categories contain 271 types of goods, including 22 textiles, 31 metal products, 67 machines and appliances, 78 chemical products, 20 beverages and food, 47 sundries, and 6 others. However, the formal investigation has not yet been completed, and the actual number should be much higher. Based on this information, the government will work hard to encourage the people to purchase domestic products and hopes that the people will cooperate with the government to achieve this goal. The great cause of promoting domestic industries cannot be achieved by the government alone, and the whole people must unanimously support the government to succeed.

We Japanese people are slack and have developed extremely extravagant lifestyles, blindly estimating the value of foreign goods without realizing the severity of the domestic economic slump and the danger to the country's future. At this moment, we Japanese must rise up together, love and use domestic products to promote industry and increase national wealth. However, loving and using domestic products does not mean using all domestic products of inferior quality. The quality of domestic products that are poor must be improved. The issue of using domestic products is fundamentally an economic issue. Promoting the use of domestic products without regard to their quality and value is inappropriate. Therefore, Japanese manufacturers should pay attention to the issue of quality and value and strive to make them cheap and of good quality to compete with foreign goods. On the one hand, consumers should consider that the development of domestic products is greatly related to the future of national wealth and strength, and even if there is a temporary sacrifice, they should not care, but only use domestic products. If so, the improvement of domestic product output will be constantly improving.

Siamese Minister of Commerce to Travel to China, Japan, and India

Switzerland Enacts New Law to Prevent Tuberculosis

Some Criticize it as Interfering with Personal Freedom

Geneva News: The Swiss government is now implementing a federal law to prevent tuberculosis throughout the country. The content is extremely strict. Doctors must report every tuberculosis case to the local authorities in order to prevent its spread. If a deceased patient has contact with living people, doctors must announce whether the patient's death was due to tuberculosis. All public institutions are subject to this new law. School teachers, nannies, and students must undergo medical examinations. Any suspicious houses will be inspected by public groups. If they are found to be infected with germs, they will be prohibited from being inhabited. Anyone who does not comply with this law will be subject to heavy fines. Some criticize this new law as interfering with citizens' personal freedom, while others believe it is a sound law to eradicate tuberculosis and protect health.

New Hygiene Movement Underway in France

The Goal is "Preventing Disease Before it Happens"

University Professor Believes That Disease Can Be Completely Eliminated

France has a major new movement underway to promote health and eliminate disease. Its main purpose can be summarized in one sentence: "Preventing disease before it happens."

This movement began last year in Strasbourg, Alsace, when the Dean of Strasbourg University ordered that all medical students at the school undergo a detailed physical examination by a doctor at the beginning of their studies, and be subjected to several X-rays to check whether their bodies are healthy. The purpose of this measure is: "These students will all be engaged in medicine in the future, and are more likely to come into contact with patients than anyone else, so they need great physical resistance. Since they are going to be asked to treat the diseases of others, they should also know how to treat their own diseases. Since they must warn others, they should also know how to warn themselves."

A total of 97 medical students at the school (including 11 female students) were examined, and it was found that 24 of them were suffering from illnesses, but they were either unaware of them, or although aware, did not know their severity. Four-fifths of them found their teeth unhealthy as a result of local examinations. All students who have been examined are of course allowed to enter the school to study, but they are warned about their physical weaknesses so that they know to be cautious. This is to guide them on their path in life.

This trial method was heard by the Director-General of Education of the French government, who greatly appreciated it and decided to extend it to all public and private schools. Since January of this year, a middle school in Paris has followed this method, and all male and female students have been subjected to the same examination, which is repeated every three months. The school printed a small book called "Health Record" and distributed it to the students. The book records the results of each examination, and also measures the students' physical fitness on a regular basis, so that the extent to which physical exercise is appropriate and what kind of exercise is most beneficial is also listed in the book. There are various benefits to this method: (1) If the student is ill, the doctor can know his usual shortcomings from this when the family asks a doctor for treatment, (2) The physical education teacher in the school can use this to teach, (3) When the students enter middle school or university in the future, the school authorities can also know the physical condition of each student from this and pay attention to them separately. In short, this method has advantages and no disadvantages.

French scientists are all enthusiastic about this trial. For example, Professor Mazhoge of the Paris Pasteur Institute said, "It is far easier to prevent disease than to treat it. Looking around us, we hear about illnesses and suffering every day, and medicine has lost its authority, but if we pay attention to it early, the disease can be prevented. The biggest mistake is not knowing hygiene, listening to nature, and then crying in pain when the disease occurs, which is too late. If we can examine on a regular basis, we can find the enemy of health in its hiding place."

Another scientist, Mr. Xilaban, said, "Hygiene methods are negative. They only tell you what not to do and what mistakes should be avoided. Conversely, preventive treatment methods are positive. They tell you in advance what must be done to protect your health from harm. Engines, automobiles, and elevators are all checked daily. How can human organs not be examined on a regular basis? Professor Meeklin of Strasbourg University most appreciated this method and said, "In my opinion, I am certain that one day the world will completely eliminate disease, and people will only die of old age and not of disease."

New Substitute for Steam

Steam has great uses in modern civilization, but the method is still too clumsy and there is a risk of explosion, so scientists are still tirelessly seeking a substitute. Now, success has been achieved.

The new substance is called Heat Transte, scientifically known as Diphenyl, which is a chemical combination product that does not exist in its original state. It contains a great amount of heat and there is no danger of excessive steam pressure. At a temperature of 700 degrees, Heat Transte only has a pressure of 65 pounds, while steam has more than 1,000 pounds.

Two years ago, an oil merchant wanted to use the substance to replace steam in the work of refining gasoline, but was unsuccessful. At that time, there was only one pound of Heat Transte in the United States, worth 40 yuan. Later, Theodore Swann, a young chemist from Birmingham, Alabama, manufactured it in large quantities, and now it is only worth 30 cents per pound.

Heat Transte is made by explosively cracking benzene to drive out two hydrogen atoms from the hydrocarbon and synthesizing a new substance. It is a slightly yellow, white solid that melts at 155 degrees Fahrenheit.

Heat Transte has proven to be a very useful substance. It has been made into amber-colored resin, black, and gray transparent solids, and is used in the manufacture of varnishes, insulators, fireproof products, and waterproof products. (Junshan)

Rubber Inventory for Nine Months

The Result May Be to Limit Production

The current rubber market is extremely cheap in London, New York, and Singapore. According to a survey by a certain party, the world's rubber inventory at the end of July was as follows:

Tons Tons

New York 155,000 Other 15,000

London 110,000 In Transit 90,000

Singapore 35,000 Total 405,000

Malaya 40,000

This inventory is approximately seven and a half months' worth of rubber, based on the world's total rubber demand of 710,000 tons and an average monthly demand of 60,000 tons. Deducting the total demand of 710,000 tons from this year's production of 840,000 tons leaves a surplus of 130,000 tons, which, combined with the 427,000 tons of inventory at the end of last year, will result in an inventory of approximately 559,000 tons by the end of this year, or an inventory of approximately nine months. On the one hand, the slump in the American market is gradually deepening, and the demand for rubber has not increased, but has tended to decline. The insecurity of the future is increasing, resulting in the above-mentioned low prices. Under this situation, producers and rubber dealers alike will inevitably fail. There is talk in England of limiting rubber production. The issue of production restrictions was previously advocated by Dutch growers, but no agreement was reached due to British indifference. Today, prices are extremely cheap, and this situation may lead to production restrictions.

Many Banks in the United States Close

More Than 400 Banks Closed in Five Months

New York News: According to the announcement of the Federal Reserve Board, the number of banks closed in the most recent five months was 404, with capital amounting to 139,902,000 gold dollars. Due to the deepening of the general business slump and the recent instability of early agriculture, the financial world is even more difficult. Some bankers predict that more banks will close this year, and the record of 956 banks closed in 1926 may be broken.
